        \"decodeHeaders when end_stream is already false\");\n571: \n572:     ENVOY_STREAM_LOG(trace, \"decode headers called: filter={} status={}\", *this,\n573: The empty data frame is sent\n597:     // after the new metadata.\n598:     if ((*entry)->end_stream_ && new_metadata_added && !buffered_request_data_) {\n599:       Buffer::OwnedImpl empty_data(\"\");\n600:       ENVOY_STREAM_LOG(\n601:           trace, \"inserting an empty data frame for end_stream due metadata being added.\", *this);\n602:       // Metadata frame doesn't carry end of stream bit. If it is the last filter, continue with\n609:       // processing since we need to handle the case where a terminal filter wants to buffer, but\n610:       // a previous filter has added body.\n611:       maybeContinueDecoding(continue_data_entry);\n612:       return;\n613:     }\n614: \n615:     // Here we handle the case where we have a header only request, but a filter adds a body\n616:     // to it. Just drop it.\n646:   if (stopDecoderFilterChain()) {\n647:     return;\n648:   }\n649: \n650:   auto trailers_added_entry = decoder_filters_.end();\n651:   const bool trailers_exists_at_start = filter_manager_callbacks_.requestTrailers().has_value();\n652:   // Filter iteration may start at the current filter.\n653:   StreamDecoderFilters::Iterator entry = commonDecodePrefix(filter, filter_iteration_start_state);\n654:   bool terminal_filter_decoded_end_stream = false;\n655:   ASSERT(!state_.decoder_filter_chain_complete_ || entry == decoder_filters_.end() ||\n656:          (*entry)->end_stream_);\n657: \n658:   for (; If just skip the filter, the codes after the loop will be called with\n693:     // wrong data. For encodeData, the response_encoder->encode() will be called.\n694:     if ((*entry)->end_stream_) {\n695:       return;\n696:     }\n697:     ASSERT(!(state_.filter_call_state_ & FilterCallState::EndOfStream;\n704:     }\n705: \n706:     recordLatestDataFilter(entry, state_.latest_data_decoding_filter_, decoder_filters_);\n707: \n708:     state_.filter_call_state_ |= FilterCallState::DecodeData;\n709:     (*entry)->end_stream_ = end_stream && !filter_manager_callbacks_.requestTrailers();\n710:     FilterDataStatus status = (*entry)->handle_->decodeData(data,                 (*entry)->filter_context_.config_name, static_cast<uint64_t>(status));\n720:     if (state_.decoder_filter_chain_aborted_) {\n721:       executeLocalReplyIfPrepared();\n722:       ENVOY_STREAM_LOG(trace, \"decodeData filter iteration aborted due to local reply: filter={}\",\n723:                        *this, (*entry)->filter_context_.config_name);\n724:       return;\n725: decoder_filters_.end()) {\n731:       end_stream = false;\n732:       trailers_added_entry = entry;\n733:     }\n734: \n735:     // The decoder filter chain is finished here if the following is
